FORM VI
[See rule 16 ]
DECLARATION
No. II(2)/PWD/401/2021.
Whereas it appears to the  Government that a total of 12.37.00 hectares of land is 
required in the Munanjipatti  Village in Nanguneri  Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose 
namely in Interlinking of  Tamirabarani – Karumeniyar - Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Cannal 
Project.
Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 12.37.00 hectares 
is under acquisition for the above said project in the Munanjipatti Village in Nanguneri Taluk in 
Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under Section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil. 
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Office of the Land Acquisition Officer, Office of the  Special Tahsildar (L.A), River Linking Project, Unit IV 
Nanguneri and  Office of the Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division,  Tirunelveli on any working day.

28
PUBLIC WORKS DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS.
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡. 86, ªð£¶Š ðE(ŠH&2)ˆ ¶¬ø, 4 «ñ 2021, 
CˆF¬ó 21, Hôõ, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
FORM VI
[See rule 16 ]
DECLARATION
No. II(2)/PWD/402/2021.
Whereas it appears to the  Government that a total of 12.61.11 hectares of land is required in the Moolakaraipatti part 1  Village in Nanguneri  Taluk in Tirunelveli District 
for public purpose namely, Interlinking of  Tamirabarani – Karumeniyar - Nambiyar rivers for the   Flood Carrier Cannal Project. Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that 
a piece of land measuring 12.61.11 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the  Moolakaraipatti Part 1 Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District whose 
detailed description is as follows

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under Section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the land  acquisition Officier O/o Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-2, Nanguneri and 
O/o  Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division,  Ambasamudram  on any working day.

[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡. 87, ªð£¶ŠðE(ŠH&2)ˆ ¶¬ø, 4 «ñ 2021, CˆF¬ó 21, Hôõ, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
FORM VI
[See rule 16 ]
DECLARATION
No. II(2)/PWD/403/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 4.12.5 hectare of wet land is required in the Ponnakudi Village in Palayamkottai Taluk in Tirunelveli 
District for public purpose namely, Interlinking of  Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar rivers for the   Flood Carrier Cannal Project. Now, therefore a declaration is 
made hereby that a piece of land measuring 4.12.5 hectare of wet land is under acquisition for the above said project in the Ponnakudi Village in Palayamkottai 
Taluk in Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

4.12.5
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair 
Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be 
resettled due to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Land Acquisition Officer i.e Office of the  Special Tahsildar(L.A), River Link Project(Unit-III), 
Palayamkottai and  Office of the  Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Ambasamudram  on any working day.

FORM VI
[See Rule 16 ]
DECLARATION
No. II(2)/PWD/404/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 22.43.50 hectare of land is required in the Melathidiyur Village in Palayamkottai Taluk in Tirunelveli 
District for public purpose namely , Interlinking of Tamirabarani- Karumeniyar- Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Cannal Project.Now, therefore a declaration 
is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 22.43.5 hectare is under acquisition for the above said project in the Melathidiyur Village in Palayamkottai Taluk 
in Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Land Acquisition Officer i.e Office of the  Special Tahsildar(L.A), River Link Project (Unit-III), 
Palayamkottai and  Office of the  Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli  on any working day,

FORM VI
[SEE RULE 16 ]
DECLARATION
No. II(2)/IPWD/405/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 0.25.0 hectare of land is required in the Kuravarkulam Village in Palayamkottai Taluk in Tirunelveli 
District for public purpose namely , Interlinking of Tamirabarani- Nambiyar - Karumeniyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Cannal Project. Now, therefore a declaration 
is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 0.25.0 hectare is under acquisition for the above said project in the Kuravarkulam Village in Palayamkottai 
Taluk in Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under Section 15 of the Right to Fair 
Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely 
to be resettled due to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the 
mines and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the 
land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Land Acquisition Officer i.e Office of the Special Tahsildar(L.A), River Link Project(Unit-III), 
Palayamkottai and Office of the Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli on any working day.

Total
16.54.98
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under Section 15 of the Right to Fair 
Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely 
to be resettled due to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the 
mines and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the 
land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Office of the Land Acquisition Officer i.e Office of the Special Tahsildar (L.A), River Link Project 
(Unit-III), Palayamkottai and Office of the Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli on any working day.

[G.O.Ms. No. 91, Public Works (P2), 4 «ñ 2021, CˆF¬ó 21, Hôõ, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052]
FORM VI
[See rule 16 ]
DECLARATION
No. II(2)/PWD/407/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 40.14.72 hectare of land is required in the Cherankovilpathu Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Tirunelveli District 
for public purpose namely , Interlinking of  Tamirabarani- Karumeniyar- Nambiyar rivers for the   flood carrier cannal project.
Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 40.14.72 hectare is under acquisition for the above said project in the Cherankovilpathu 
Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

116/5, 6

Total
40.14.72
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to 
Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely 
to be resettled due to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals 
which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Land Acquisition Officer i.e Office of the  Special Tahsildar(L.A), River Link Project(Unit-I), 
Ambasamudram @ Cheranmahadevi  and  Office of the  Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli  on any working day
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
        K.MANIVASAN,
                                                                                                                               Principal Secretary to Government.
